GT: F0*sin(t) - alpha*v**c0 - omega0**c1*(gamma*Abs(v)**c2 + c3)*x - omega0**c4*x
Candidate formulas: 54

GT (fully expanded) is
\[
-0.0230405406738805\,v^3\;-\;1.1056075693807\,x\,(0.0552411020531317|v|^{1/3}+1)\;-\;1.1056075693807\,x\;+\;0.350781823399691\sin(t).
\]
Combine the two linear-in-\(x\) pieces:
\[
-1.1056075693807\,x(0.0552411|v|^{1/3}+1)\;-\;1.1056075693807x
=-(1.1056075693807\cdot 0.0552411)\,x|v|^{1/3}\;-\;2.2112151387614\,x.
\]
So GT is exactly of the form
\[
A\sin(t)+B v^3 + C x + D\,x|v|^{1/3}
\]
with fixed constants \(A=0.350781823399691\), \(B=-0.0230405406738805\), \(C=-2.2112151387614\), \(D=-(1.1056075693807\cdot 0.0552411020531317)\).

Now check candidates: any candidate that can be reduced (by setting extra parameters to 0) to
\[
(\text{linear }x) + (\text{sin/cos in }t) + (\text{}v^3) + (x|v|^{1/3})
\]
can match, provided the trig term can be phase-shifted from cos to sin.

Key trig fact: \(\cos(t-\pi/2)=\sin(t)\). So any \(c1\cos(c2+t)\) can match \(0.35078\sin(t)\) by choosing \(c1=0.35078\) and \(c2=-\pi/2\) (mod \(2\pi\)).

**GT:** `-0.0230405406738805*v**3 - 1.1056075693807*x*(0.0552411020531317*Abs(v)**0.333333333333333 + 1) - 1.1056075693807*x + 0.350781823399691*sin(t)`

Let me expand this:
- `-0.0230405406738805*v**3`
- `-1.1056075693807*x*0.0552411020531317*Abs(v)**(1/3) - 1.1056075693807*x`
- `-1.1056075693807*x`
- `+0.350781823399691*sin(t)`

So GT = `-2.2112151387614*x - 0.0610834778498*x*Abs(v)**(1/3) - 0.0230405406738805*v**3 + 0.350781823399691*sin(t)`

Note: `sin(t) = cos(t - ŽĆ/2)`, so `c1*cos(c2 + t)` can match `sin(t)` by setting `c2 = -ŽĆ/2`.

The GT has exactly these terms:
1. `c*x` (linear in x)
2. `c*x*Abs(v)**(1/3)`
3. `c*v**3`
4. `c*sin(t)` equivalently `c*cos(t + phase)`

Now I'll check each candidate:

The last term `c5*x*Max(0, c6+Abs(x))` cannot be zeroed without losing generality (setting c5=0 removes it, but then we have the base 4 terms). With c5=0, this becomes Candidate 34. Let me check if c5=0 works - yes, it gives the 4 base terms. So this matches with c5=0.
